傭兵帝国。聖堂騎士団。軍隊派遣会社……　通称〝武帝〟。
Mercenary Empire. Knights Templar. Military dispatch company …… Commonly known as “Wudi”.

その集団は北曾西南、渡島半島から西へ海を隔てて五〇キロ程の、松前大島を根城とする。　海産物の豊富な環境であるが、彼らは漁業に関心を示すことがなかった。
The group is based on Matsumae Oshima, which is about 50 kilometers west of the Oshima Peninsula in the southwestern part of Hokuso. Although the environment is rich in marine products, they have shown no interest in fishing.

彼らの生業は戦争である。
Their livelihood is war.

近隣を切り従え、領土を広げようとするのではない。　そうした侵略を望む者に、又はその侵略を防ごうとする者に、雇われて戦うのだ。
It does not try to cut down on the neighborhood and expand its territory. It is hired and fought by those who desire such aggression, or those who try to prevent it.

彼らは理非を問わない。国家を問わず民族を問わず宗教も主義主張も一切問わない。　契約条件が満たされるか否か。雇用の諾否を決するのはその一事のみである。
They make no sense. Regardless of nation or ethnicity, religion or principle is not considered. Whether the contract conditions are met. That is the only thing that decides whether to accept or reject employment.

条件はやや、特殊なものであったが。　金銭面から見る限り、彼らが雇用者へ提供する戦力は値に対して全く破格と云えたろう。
Although the conditions were a little special. From a financial point of view, the force they provide to their employers is totally unprecedented in value.

〝武帝〟の戦闘力の中心は、真打劒冑を有する武者が担う。
The center of the fighting power of "Wudi" is the warrior who has a true helmet.

高速徹甲弾、発振砲等、対竜騎兵用狙撃兵器の発達に伴って数打劒冑と真打劒冑の力関係は劇的な逆転を遂げた。　最新の兵器は、真打の古い統御機能では扱えない。
With the development of anti-dragoon sniper weapons such as high-speed armor-piercing shells and oscillating cannons, the power relationship between several and true helmets has undergone a dramatic reversal. The latest weapons cannot be handled by the old control function of the true hit.

白兵戦を表芸とする真打武者にとって、栄光は過去のものとなった。　数打劒冑を雑器、安物、紛い物と、嗤っていられた時代は永遠に過ぎ去ったのだ。
Glory is a thing of the past for hand-to-hand combat warriors. The era of slaughtered helmets as miscellaneous goods, cheap goods, and mischievous things has passed forever.

それでも彼らの多くは騎士階級、つまり前線で戦うよりも指揮統率を任務とする者であったから、軍隊に居場所を全く失ったわけではない。　最強の実戦力とは見做されなくなっただけである。
Still, many of them were knights, who were more commanding and commanding than fighting on the front lines, so they didn't lose their place in the military at all. It is no longer regarded as the strongest actual force.

しかし、最強戦力たる自負こそは彼らの軍指揮権に、延いては階級意識に正当性を与える根拠であったため、数打武者の台頭に耐えられず、逃げるように軍籍から離れた者は少なくなかった。
However, since the pride of being the strongest force was the basis for giving legitimacy to their military command and, by extension, class consciousness, few people could not stand the rise of several strikers and left the military register to escape. There wasn't.

そんな逸れ武者を〝武帝〟は受け入れ……　そして、彼らに自己認識を取り戻させた。
"Wudi" accepted such a deviant warrior ... and made them regain their self-awareness.

正面戦闘の優位を数打に譲ろうと、真打武者は未だ強猛な存在には違いない。　彼らの多くは高い性能、熟練の技術、豊富な経験を兼ね備える。
The true hit warrior must still be a ferocious player, trying to give up the advantage of frontal combat to a few hits. Many of them have high performance, skill and abundant experience.

一騎で重戦車の隊列を相手取り、砲兵陣地を砕くも困難としない。　いや最新の竜騎兵さえ、状況と戦術を選んで格闘戦に持ち込めば互角以上に戦える――むしろ圧倒できる。
It's not difficult to crush the artillery position against a platoon of heavy tanks with one horse. No, even the latest dragoons can fight more than equal if they choose the situation and tactics and bring them into the fight-rather overwhelming.

運用の仕方を誤らねば、多大な戦果を挙げ得るのだ。　　つまり〝武帝〟はそうして、両者の要望に応えた。誇りを求める武者と、力を求める依頼者の。
If you don't use it incorrectly, you can achieve great results. In other words, "Wudi" then responded to the requests of both parties. A warrior who seeks pride and a client who seeks power.

俄かに出現した孤島の傭兵団が短時日で名を成した所以はここにある。
This is the reason why the mercenary corps of the isolated island that appeared suddenly made a name in a short time.

広く知られてゆくにつれ、〝武帝〟への依頼は数を増やした――その陰惨な契約条件にも関わらず。　大和で、大陸で、あるいは更に遠方で。彼らは頼まれるまま数多の戦闘に加わり、勝利と死を積み重ねた。
As it became widely known, the number of requests to "Wudi" increased-despite its gruesome terms and conditions. In Yamato, on the continent, or even farther away. They participated in numerous battles as requested, winning and dying.

大和や露帝がこの剣呑な不法占拠者を松前大島から追い出そうと兵を繰り出すこともあったが……　その試みは毎回、あたかも重力の働きが狂ったかのような異様な嵐に阻まれ、頓挫している。
Yamato and the Russian Emperor sometimes sent out soldiers to expel this swordsman illegal occupant from Matsumae Oshima, but every attempt was hampered by a strange storm as if the work of gravity had gone mad. ing.

海上交通を妨げる意図が見えないこともあり、昨今は両国も〝武帝〟の存在を消極的に承認しつつあった。　非公式には――時として積極的に利用することさえも。
Nowadays, both countries are reluctantly approving the existence of "Wu Emperor" because the intention to obstruct maritime traffic cannot be seen. Informally-sometimes even actively using it.

かくして傭兵帝国は極東に立つ。　混沌窮まる情勢の渦中を縦横無尽に駆け巡り、戦い、殺し――そうする中で更に武威を高め、存在感を高め、名の持つ圧力を高めながら。
Thus the mercenary empire stands in the Far East. Riding, fighting, and killing in the midst of a chaotic situation-increasing the power, presence, and pressure of the name.

頼り縋る者を日毎に増やしながら。　忌み嫌う者をも、同じ速さで増やしながら。
While increasing the number of people who rely on us day by day. While increasing the number of people who hate it at the same speed.

どうも酷く警戒されているようだ。　旧来住民との間柄が良くなく、衝突も発生している現状では無理からぬ態度だが……といって、このまま見合っていても埒は明かない。
It seems that he is very cautious. It's not unreasonable in the current situation where the relationship with the old residents is not good and there are conflicts.

こちらから呼び掛けてみるか？　この空気ではかえって警戒を深めさせる結果になりかねないが、しかし――
Would you like to call from here? This air can result in deeper vigilance, but--

「あれ……あんた」
"That ... you"

「……？」
"...?"

A young man looked into his face from behind the house. After looking at me, I tilted my head once to look for my memory and looked at me again.

「…………」
“…………”

A painful gaze and words pierced from behind in exactly the same way as the previous voice, but I will repair the wind that I do not notice. Anyway, this was a strange currency.

「その節はお騒がせしました」

言いかけて、逡巡する。　話を聞くには聞くなりの立場を示さねばならないが……彼に対して警官という名乗りは有効だろうか？
Call and crawl. To hear the story, you have to show your position, but ... is it valid to call him a policeman?

おそらく単純に好意では迎えられまい。　とはいえ、警察を自称しないのであれば俺の立場は昨日の酔漢のままである。まともに相手をして貰えるとは思えなかった。
Perhaps simply not welcomed by favor. However, if I don't call myself the police, my position remains yesterday's drunkard. I didn't think I would get a decent partner.

……止む無し。
...... There is no stopping.

案の定だった。　若い男の表情が露骨に引き攣り、周囲の押し殺した気配もざわりと波立つ。
Sure enough. The expression of the young man is blatantly cramped, and the signs of being killed by the surroundings are also rippling.

法制上、正規の鎌倉市民とは言えない彼らにとって、警察は保護者ではないのだ。　むしろ逆だろう――その点の危惧を拭うため、俺はすぐ言葉を継いだ。
The police are not guardians for those who are not legal Kamakura citizens. Rather the opposite-I immediately took over the words to dispel concerns about that.

巧言を弄んでも自分の胸が苦しくなるだけだ。　俺は正直なところを答えた。
Playing with clever words only makes my chest painful. I answered honestly.

実際、軍あるいは警察がそうした短絡的措置で難民問題の解決を図る事は充分に有り得る。
In fact, it is quite possible that the military or police will try to solve the refugee problem with such short-circuit measures.

つまりこの難民キャンプは、近畿東海で展開される今川雷蝶と足利幸行の抗争に逐われた人々の集まりか。　六波羅の主権を競う激闘で住処を奪われ、鎌倉まで逃げ延びてきたというわけだ。
In other words, is this refugee camp a group of people who were driven by the conflict between Raichou Imakawa and Yukiyuki Ashikaga in the Kinki Tokai region? In a fierce battle for Rokuhara's sovereignty, he was robbed of his place of residence and fled to Kamakura.

彼らにはもはや帰る所も行く所も無いだろう。

A man who shrugs and answers. There was no need to ask, it was a matter of course.

要するに、正規の市民の間でも広がっている問題が彼らにはより深刻な問題として存在するという事だ。　……この解決は俺の能力の及ぶところではなかった。将来的な行政に期待するほかない。
The bottom line is that problems that are widespread among legitimate citizens exist as more serious problems for them. ...... This solution was beyond my ability. I have no choice but to look forward to future administration.

俺にできるのは、もっと小さな事だろう。
What I can do is something smaller.

「旧来の住民との間にトラブルがあるという話も聞いていますが」

昼。　再び光の家へ食料を持参し、ついでに自分の食事も済ませる。
Noon. Bring food to the House of Light again and finish your meal as well.

大した物ではなかったが、朝と同様、家主は素直に喜んでくれた様子であった。　嬉しく思う一方、これまでどんな食生活だったのか不安にもなる。
It wasn't a big deal, but as in the morning, the landlord seemed to be obediently pleased. While I'm happy, I'm also worried about what kind of eating habits I've had so far.

Relationships can be broken in an instant, but reconciliation may not be achieved even after 100 years.

The man who visited me again welcomed me with a look of another. A few others are appearing behind it, perhaps with some diminished vigilance.

半分以上は勘だが、その点には同意できた。　おそらく橋を壊したのは全く別の人間だろう。

鎌倉署長は公人として必ずしも甘い温情家ではない。　が、難民対策を決めるに当たって、もし『住民との良好な関係』という一事実があるのなら、決して軽視はしない筈だった。
Chief Kamakura is not necessarily a sweet sympathizer as a public figure. However, when deciding on refugee measures, if there was one fact of "good relations with the residents," it should never be underestimated.

村正は大工ではないが、劒冑の異能を行使できる。　橋の再建に役立つ事は間違いないだろう。　　しかし、作業仲間にどう説明したものか。
Muramasa is not a carpenter, but he can exercise his abilities. There is no doubt that it will help rebuild the bridge. But how did you explain it to your colleagues?

一介の警官が劒冑を持つ筈はない。　強引に言い繕えば不審を買い、折角まとまった話も水泡に帰す恐れがある。
A policeman cannot have a helmet. If you forcibly rephrase it, you may buy suspicious things, and even a well-organized story may be blisters.

資材の調達は滞りなく済んだ。　その翌日、早速作業を開始する。
Procurement of materials was completed without delay. The next day, work will start immediately.

集まった人員は総勢六人。　本当はもう少し手が欲しいところだったが、贅沢を言っても仕方ない。
A total of six people gathered. I really wanted a little more, but I can't help saying luxury.

まずは現場の検分から始める。
First, start with on-site inspection.

Within minutes of entering the river, I could see why it wasn't a children's playground. It's too dangerous.

深い上に川底はぬかるみ、しかも流れは速い。　重要な橋というわりに即席の浮橋を仕立てて代用にする様子がないのも、この川並なら当然だった。
It is deep and the riverbed is muddy, and the flow is fast. It was natural for this Kawanami that there was no sign of tailoring an instant pontoon bridge instead of an important bridge.

雪車町一蔵は去り、
Sorimachi Ichizo is gone,

大鳥香奈枝は待ち、
Kanae Otori waits,

綾弥一条は、行く。
Ayaya Ichijo goes.

風が一陣、流れた。
A breeze blew.

そこに紛れる猛気が、肌を炙る。　俺は振り返った。
The fierceness that is lost there burns the skin. I looked back.

良く知る少女が立っている。　濃藍の劒冑を従えて、夕闇の下。
A girl who knows well is standing. Under the dusk, accompanied by a dark indigo helmet.

今、俺へ向ける顔にあるものは――
What's on my face right now--

怒り。
anger.

「…………」
“…………”

一語も交わさず、避けられぬ戦いの到来を感じ取り。　俺の口が苦く歪んで――
Feeling the arrival of the inevitable battle without exchanging a word. My mouth is bitter and distorted--

違う。　こうでは、ないな。
Wrong. This is not the case.

戦いに臨む悪鬼の貌は、こうではない。
The appearance of the devil who faces the battle is not like this.

俺は今から、俺自身が求めた闘争へ身を投じるのだ。　苦る理由が何処にあろうか。
From now on, I will devote myself to the struggle I have sought. Where is the reason for suffering?

表情は、こうだ。　こう――
The expression is like this. like this--

現れた敵対者が装甲を遂げる。　俺も追う。
The adversary who appears achieves armor. I will follow you too.

誓いの言葉を唱え。　その銘を呼び。
Recite the word of oath. Call that inscription.

我が肉体を鉄とする――――
Let my body be iron ――――

「おい、てめぇら作業はどうしたんだよ?」
"Hey, what's wrong with your work?"

"... Huh?"

「橋だよ、さっさと完成させろ！」
"It's a bridge, complete it quickly!"

「知るか！　お前らで勝手にやれ！」
"Do you know! Do it yourself!"

「何ぃ?」
"What?"

「だめっ」
"No"

「……あ？」
"……Ah?"

「光坊？」
"Kobo?"

「けんか、だめ」
"Fight, no"
